### [149] [The Discrete Charm of the MLP: Binary Routing of Continuous Signals in Transformer Feed-Forward Layers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10985)
*Peter Balogh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究发现Transformer语言模型中的MLP层执行连续信号的二元路由：特定神经元形成共识架构，决定token是否需要非线性处理，这种二元路由结构解释了为什么平滑多项式近似会失败。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Transformer语言模型中MLP层的实际工作机制，理解其如何处理连续信号并做出路由决策，以及为什么传统的平滑多项式近似方法无法有效描述这些高度非线性层的行为。

Method: 分析GPT-2 Small模型，识别MLP层中的二元路由机制，通过交叉层分析揭示发展轨迹，进行因果验证（移除MLP对比性能影响），比较二元与连续特征的信息损失，测试多项式拟合效果。

Result: 发现MLP层实现二元路由：特定神经元形成共识架构（7个"默认开启"神经元和1个异常处理器），路由决策的二元化几乎不损失信息（准确率79.2% vs 78.8%），移除MLP在共识崩溃时导致43.3%困惑度损失，而完全共识时仅10.1%损失。多项式拟合效果极差（R²≤0.06）。

Conclusion: 深度网络的逐段仿射特性可以补充路由特性：沿着自然数据流形，分段边界实现了关于哪些token需要非线性处理的二元决策，将连续信号路由到不同的计算路径。这解释了为什么平滑近似方法失败，并提供了理解Transformer内部机制的新视角。

Abstract: We show that MLP layers in transformer language models perform binary routing of continuous signals: the decision of whether a token needs nonlinear processing is well-captured by binary neuron activations, even though the signals being routed are continuous. In GPT-2 Small (124M parameters), we find that specific neurons implement a consensus architecture -- seven "default-ON" neurons and one exception handler (N2123 in Layer 11) that are 93-98% mutually exclusive -- creating a binary routing switch. A cross-layer analysis reveals a developmental arc: early layers (L1-3) use single gateway neurons to route exceptions without consensus quorums; middle layers (L4-6) show diffuse processing with neither gateway nor consensus; and late layers (L7-11) crystallize full consensus/exception architectures with increasing quorum size (1 to 3 to 7 consensus neurons). Causal validation confirms the routing is functional: removing the MLP at consensus breakdown costs 43.3% perplexity, while at full consensus removing it costs only 10.1% -- exceeding a 4x difference. Comparing binary vs. continuous features for the routing decision confirms that binarization loses essentially no information (79.2% vs. 78.8% accuracy), while continuous activations carry additional magnitude information (R^2 = 0.36 vs. 0.22). This binary routing structure explains why smooth polynomial approximation fails: cross-validated polynomial fits (degrees 2-7) never exceed R^2 = 0.06 for highly nonlinear layers. We propose that the well-established piecewise-affine characterization of deep networks can be complemented by a routing characterization: along the natural data manifold, the piecewise boundaries implement binary decisions about which tokens need nonlinear processing, routing continuous signals through qualitatively different computational paths.

</details>

*Heikki Haario,Zhi-Song Liu,Martin Simon,Hendrik Weichel*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法在参数不确定性量化时需要准确的先验分布，而直接筛选或随机采样模型参数会导致训练时间过长，且可能在不物理的参数值上进行评估。本文研究相反情况，即如何在不准确先验分布下进行高效的不确定性量化。

Method: 将不确定性量化与网络架构解耦，不采样网络权重，而是通过马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）将模型参数分布作为输入引入网络训练。该方法与神经网络选择完全无关，提出了分位数模拟器和基于自编码器的ODE网络模拟器。

Result: 代理模型能够实现与底层物理模型相同的不确定性量化，但计算时间显著减少。提出的方法能够灵活估计不同ODE模型参数对应的不同轨迹路径。

Conclusion: 通过数学分析提供了透明的方式，将潜在性能损失与可测量的分布不匹配联系起来。该方法为在缺乏准确先验分布情况下进行高效不确定性量化提供了新思路。

Abstract: Neural networks are a commonly used approach to replace physical models with computationally cheap surrogates. Parametric uncertainty quantification can be included in training, assuming that an accurate prior distribution of the model parameters is available. Here we study the common opposite situation, where direct screening or random sampling of model parameters leads to exhaustive training times and evaluations at unphysical parameter values. Our solution is to decouple uncertainty quantification from network architecture. Instead of sampling network weights, we introduce the model-parameter distribution as an input to network training via Markov chain Monte Carlo (MCMC). In this way, the surrogate achieves the same uncertainty quantification as the underlying physical model, but with substantially reduced computation time. The approach is fully agnostic with respect to the neural network choice. In our examples, we present a quantile emulator for prediction and a novel autoencoder-based ODE network emulator that can flexibly estimate different trajectory paths corresponding to different ODE model parameters. Moreover, we present a mathematical analysis that provides a transparent way to relate potential performance loss to measurable distribution mismatch.

</details>


### [151] [Factorized Neural Implicit DMD for Parametric Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10995)
*Siyuan Chen,Zhecheng Wang,Yixin Chen,Yue Chang,Peter Yichen Chen,Eitan Grinspun,Jonathan Panuelos*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统数值求解器在高维状态空间和非线性动态系统中计算成本高，不适合实时分析和控制。即使有物理先验知识（如偏微分方程），也需要数据驱动、无模型的方法来建模物理系统的时间演化。

Method: 提出物理编码神经场参数化的Koopman算子谱分解方法。与物理约束神经场（拟合单个解曲面）和神经算子（在固定时间范围近似解算子）不同，该方法学习分解的流算子，将空间模式和时间演化解耦，揭示底层特征值、模式和稳定性。

Result: 在多种动态系统问题上验证了方法的有效性，能够准确预测复杂的时空现象，同时提供系统动态行为的洞察，支持稳定的长期推演、参数空间插值和谱分析。

Conclusion: 该方法通过学习Koopman算子的谱分解，实现了对动态系统参数化流的高效建模，为复杂物理系统的实时分析和控制提供了有力工具。

Abstract: A data-driven, model-free approach to modeling the temporal evolution of physical systems mitigates the need for explicit knowledge of the governing equations. Even when physical priors such as partial differential equations are available, such systems often reside in high-dimensional state spaces and exhibit nonlinear dynamics, making traditional numerical solvers computationally expensive and ill-suited for real-time analysis and control. Consider the problem of learning a parametric flow of a dynamical system: with an initial field and a set of physical parameters, we aim to predict the system's evolution over time in a way that supports long-horizon rollouts, generalization to unseen parameters, and spectral analysis.
  We propose a physics-coded neural field parameterization of the Koopman operator's spectral decomposition. Unlike a physics-constrained neural field, which fits a single solution surface, and neural operators, which directly approximate the solution operator at fixed time horizons, our model learns a factorized flow operator that decouples spatial modes and temporal evolution. This structure exposes underlying eigenvalues, modes, and stability of the underlying physical process to enable stable long-term rollouts, interpolation across parameter spaces, and spectral analysis. We demonstrate the efficacy of our method on a range of dynamics problems, showcasing its ability to accurately predict complex spatiotemporal phenomena while providing insights into the system's dynamic behavior.

</details>


### [152] [Cross-Species Transfer Learning for Electrophysiology-to-Transcriptomics Mapping in Cortical GABAergic Interneurons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11000)
*Theo Schwider,Ramin Ramezani*

TL;DR: 该研究复制并扩展了Gouwens等人的电生理-转录组学框架，使用小鼠和人类皮层Patch-seq数据，开发了基于注意力的BiLSTM模型，实现了跨物种迁移学习，提升了人类神经元亚类预测性能。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单细胞电生理记录是研究神经元功能多样性的重要工具，但如何将电生理特征与转录组身份联系起来仍具挑战。本研究旨在复制并扩展Gouwens等人建立的框架，利用公开的Allen Institute数据，开发更优的跨物种分析方法。

Abstract: Single-cell electrophysiological recordings provide a powerful window into neuronal functional diversity and offer an interpretable route for linking intrinsic physiology to transcriptomic identity. Here, we replicate and extend the electrophysiology-to-transcriptomics framework introduced by Gouwens et al. (2020) using publicly available Allen Institute Patch-seq datasets from both mouse and human cortex. We focus on GABAergic inhibitory interneurons to target a subclass structure (Lamp5, Pvalb, Sst, Vip) that is comparable and conserved across species. After quality control, we analyzed 3,699 mouse visual cortex neurons and 506 human neocortical neurons from neurosurgical resections. Using standardized electrophysiological features and sparse PCA, we reproduced the major class-level separations reported in the original mouse study. For supervised prediction, a class-balanced random forest provided a strong feature-engineered baseline in mouse data and a reduced but still informative baseline in human data. We then developed an attention-based BiLSTM that operates directly on the structured IPFX feature-family representation, avoiding sPCA and providing feature-family-level interpretability via learned attention weights. Finally, we evaluated a cross-species transfer setting in which the sequence model is pretrained on mouse data and fine-tuned on human data for an aligned 4-class task, improving human macro-F1 relative to a human-only training baseline. Together, these results confirm reproducibility of the Gouwens pipeline in mouse data, demonstrate that sequence models can match feature-engineered baselines, and show that mouse-to-human transfer learning can provide measurable gains for human subclass prediction.

### [153] [Leech Lattice Vector Quantization for Efficient LLM Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11021)
*Tycho F. A. van der Ouderaa,Mart van Baalen,Paul Whatmough,Markus Nagel*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LLVQ使用Leech晶格进行向量量化，通过索引转换、角度搜索和并行化实现高效LLM压缩，性能超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标量量化受信息论限制，向量量化能突破这些限制但需要昂贵的查找机制。晶格方法通过结构化密集包装解决此问题，Leech晶格在24维具有最优球体包装特性，适合LLM量化。

Method: 扩展基于扩展Golay码的搜索算法：1) 支持索引，无需物化码本即可进行比特串转换；2) 允许在Leech晶格壳层联合上进行角度搜索；3) 提出完全并行化的反量化核。这些组成LLVQ算法。

Result: LLVQ在LLM量化方面达到最先进性能，超越Quip#、QTIP和PVQ等近期方法，展示了高维晶格在可扩展、理论基础的模型压缩中的重要性。

Conclusion: Leech晶格向量量化为LLM压缩提供了实用算法，证明了高维晶格在理论基础的模型压缩中的价值，为可扩展量化提供了新方向。

Abstract: Scalar quantization of large language models (LLMs) is fundamentally limited by information-theoretic bounds. While vector quantization (VQ) overcomes these limits by encoding blocks of parameters jointly, practical implementations must avoid the need for expensive lookup mechanisms or other explicit codebook storage. Lattice approaches address this through highly structured and dense packing. This paper explores the Leech lattice, which, with its optimal sphere packing and kissing configurations at 24 dimensions, is the highest dimensional lattice known with such optimal properties. To make the Leech lattice usable for LLM quantization, we extend an existing search algorithm based on the extended Golay code construction, to i) support indexing, enabling conversion to and from bitstrings without materializing the codebook, ii) allow angular search over union of Leech lattice shells, iii) propose fully-parallelisable dequantization kernel. Together this yields a practical algorithm, namely Leech Lattice Vector Quantization (LLVQ). LLVQ delivers state-of-the-art LLM quantization performance, outperforming recent methods such as Quip\#, QTIP, and PVQ. These results highlight the importance of high-dimensional lattices for scalable, theoretically grounded model compression.

</details>


### [154] [Neural Field Thermal Tomography: A Differentiable Physics Framework for Non-Destructive Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11045)
*Tao Zhong,Yixun Hu,Dongzhe Zheng,Aditya Sood,Christine Allen-Blanchette*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: NeFTY是一个可微分物理框架，用于从瞬态表面温度测量中定量重建材料属性的3D分布。它通过神经场参数化3D扩散率，利用可微分物理求解器作为硬约束，解决了传统热成像和PINNs在瞬态扩散场景中的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统热成像方法依赖像素级1D近似，忽略了横向扩散；而基于软约束的物理信息神经网络（PINNs）在瞬态扩散场景中由于梯度刚度问题经常失败。需要一种能够精确重建材料3D属性并有效处理逆热传导问题的方法。

Method: NeFTY将3D扩散率场参数化为连续神经场，通过可微分物理求解器进行优化。采用"先离散化后优化"的范式，将热力学定律作为硬约束，同时保持高分辨率3D层析所需的内存效率。

Result: 在合成数据上的实验验证表明，NeFTY在亚表面缺陷定位精度上显著优于基线方法。该方法能够有效恢复任意尺度的亚表面缺陷，解决了逆热传导问题的谱偏差和不适定性。

Conclusion: NeFTY提供了一个可微分物理框架，能够从瞬态表面温度测量中精确重建材料属性的3D分布，在热成像和材料无损检测方面具有重要应用价值。

Abstract: We propose Neural Field Thermal Tomography (NeFTY), a differentiable physics framework for the quantitative 3D reconstruction of material properties from transient surface temperature measurements. While traditional thermography relies on pixel-wise 1D approximations that neglect lateral diffusion, and soft-constrained Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs) often fail in transient diffusion scenarios due to gradient stiffness, NeFTY parameterizes the 3D diffusivity field as a continuous neural field optimized through a rigorous numerical solver. By leveraging a differentiable physics solver, our approach enforces thermodynamic laws as hard constraints while maintaining the memory efficiency required for high-resolution 3D tomography. Our discretize-then-optimize paradigm effectively mitigates the spectral bias and ill-posedness inherent in inverse heat conduction, enabling the recovery of subsurface defects at arbitrary scales. Experimental validation on synthetic data demonstrates that NeFTY significantly improves the accuracy of subsurface defect localization over baselines. Additional details at https://cab-lab-princeton.github.io/nefty/

</details>

### [158] [Regular Geometries from Singular Matter in Quasi-Topological Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10110)
*Pablo Bueno,Robie A. Hennigar,Ángel J. Murcia,Aitor Vicente-Cano*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究准拓扑引力理论在耦合物质后是否仍能保持Markov极限曲率假设，即曲率是否仍能被普适尺度所限制，探索引力-物质有效理论的选择标准。

Method: 分析真空准拓扑引力的无限项作用量，研究最小耦合物质时方程的标度性质变化，建立静态球对称应力张量的充分条件以保证曲率有界，探索包含高阶曲率和电磁项的非最小耦合理论。

Result: 最小耦合会破坏真空方程的标度性质，但几何仍常保持正则；建立了保证曲率有界的充分条件，覆盖正则和奇异物质分布；非最小耦合可以恢复Markov假设，实现与质量和电荷无关的曲率普适上界。

Conclusion: 准拓扑引力耦合物质存在微妙性质，最小耦合破坏Markov假设但非最小耦合可恢复；Markov假设可作为引力-物质有效理论重整化的选择判据，对质量暴胀等物理现象有启示。

Abstract: Vacuum quasi-topological gravity with infinitely many terms in the action satisfies Markov's limiting curvature hypothesis: the spherically symmetric solutions are regular and all curvature invariants are bounded by solution-independent scales. We study how this picture changes when the theory is coupled to matter. We find that minimally coupled matter spoils the scaling properties of the vacuum equations that lead to the validity of Markov's hypothesis, but the corresponding geometries often remain regular. We make this precise by developing a set of sufficient conditions on general static, spherically symmetric stress-tensors such that the corresponding solutions have bounded curvature. These conditions cover regular matter sectors but also singular matter profiles that are sufficiently singular in a sense we quantify. Our conclusions hold independently of the matter field equations and include configurations in which matter exhibits divergent energy density and pressure at finite radius or at Killing horizons, results that may have implications for mass inflation in these models. We then explore non-minimal couplings, focusing on theories with infinite towers of higher-curvature and electromagnetic terms in the action. In this class, Markov's hypothesis can be restored: we present theories admitting a universal upper bound on curvature, independent of the mass and charge. Overall, our results highlight subtleties in coupling quasi-topological gravity to matter and suggest Markov's hypothesis as a potential selection criterion for resummed gravity-matter effective theories.

</details>

*Takamasa Kanai*

TL;DR: 研究施瓦西黑洞内部的量子动力学，发现经典奇点的"湮灭为无"行为在标准量子化中仅对特定因子排序出现，而引入广义不确定原理后该行为被抑制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究施瓦西黑洞内部在量子引力框架下的动力学，特别是经典奇点的命运和"湮灭为无"场景的鲁棒性，探索最小长度效应如何影响奇点解析机制。

Method: 使用Ashtekar-Barbero公式化，采用迷你超空间Wheeler-DeWitt量子化方法。首先分析标准薛定谔表示，然后引入广义不确定原理(GUP)通过变形正则代数来诱导最小长度效应，求解修正的Wheeler-DeWitt方程并构建局域于视界的高斯波包。

Result: 标准量子化中，"湮灭为无"行为仅对特定因子排序出现且不具普适性。引入GUP修正后，该行为被抑制，最小长度效应显著改变了量子内部动力学。

Conclusion: 最小长度效应从本质上改变了黑洞内部的量子动力学，挑战了"湮灭为无"场景作为奇点解析机制的鲁棒性，表明量子引力效应可能提供不同的奇点解析途径。

Abstract: We study the quantum dynamics of the Schwarzschild interior in the Ashtekar-Barbero formulation, focusing on the fate of the classical singularity and the annihilation-to-nothing scenario. Using minisuperspace Wheeler-DeWitt quantization, we first analyze the standard Schrödinger representation and show that the annihilation-to-nothing behavior appears only for a specific choice of factor ordering and is not generic.
  We then introduce a generalized uncertainty principle (GUP), which induces minimal-length effects through a deformation of the canonical algebra. Solving the modified Wheeler-DeWitt equation and constructing Gaussian wave packets localized at the horizon, we find that the annihilation-to-nothing behavior is suppressed once the GUP corrections are included. Our results indicate that minimal-length effects qualitatively alter the quantum interior dynamics and challenge the robustness of this scenario as a mechanism for singularity resolution.

### [161] [The moduli space of dynamical spherically symmetric black hole spacetimes and the extremal threshold](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10378)
*Yannis Angelopoulos,Christoph Kehle,Ryan Unger*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文完整描述了爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-中性标量场系统中球对称解在Reissner-Nordström黑洞家族附近的临界行为，证明了黑洞形成阈值与极值解的关系，并发现了普适的标度律和Aretakis不稳定性现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-中性标量场系统中球对称解的动力学行为，特别是在Reissner-Nordström黑洞家族附近的临界现象，理解黑洞形成阈值、极值黑洞的稳定性以及相关的标度行为。

Method: 在无限维模空间中对Reissner-Nordström家族附近的解进行局部分析，使用分岔特征初值数据的依赖域方法，定量控制近阈值解的行为，证明解空间存在C¹叶层结构。

Result: 证明了黑洞形成阈值与极值解叶层重合，发现了事件视界位置、最终面积和温度的普适标度律（临界指数1/2），揭示了Aretakis不稳定性在阈值解中的普遍存在性，以及近阈值亚极值黑洞的瞬态视界不稳定性。

Conclusion: 该研究完整描述了Reissner-Nordström黑洞家族附近的临界行为，建立了黑洞形成阈值与极值解之间的精确对应关系，揭示了普适的标度行为和稳定性特征，为理解引力坍缩中的临界现象提供了重要理论框架。

Abstract: In this paper, we give a complete description of the black hole threshold, locally near the Reissner-Nordström family, in the infinite-dimensional moduli space $\mathfrak M$ of dynamical spherically symmetric solutions to the Einstein-Maxwell-neutral scalar field system. In a neighborhood of the full Reissner-Nordström family in $\mathfrak M$, we prove the following: (i) Any solution that forms a black hole eventually decays to a Reissner-Nordström black hole. (ii) Any solution that fails to collapse into a black hole eventually becomes superextremal along null infinity and exists globally in the domain of dependence of the bifurcate characteristic initial data. (iii) The subset of this neighborhood consisting of black hole solutions admits a $C^1$ foliation by hypersurfaces of constant final charge-to-mass ratio, up to and including extremality. (iv) The mutual boundary between the set of black hole solutions and noncollapsing solutions, i.e., the black hole threshold, is the extremal leaf of the foliation. Black holes which are not on the threshold are asymptotically subextremal. Our quantitative control of near-threshold solutions allows us to prove "universal" scaling laws for the location of the event horizon and its final area and temperature (surface gravity), with critical exponent $\frac 12$. Moreover, we show that the celebrated Aretakis instability is activated for an open and dense set of threshold solutions and that generic near-threshold subextremal black holes experience a transient horizon instability on the timescale of their inverse final temperature.

</details>

Method: 使用Legendre变换建立哈密顿动力学，在几何动力学和杨-米尔斯型表示中描述系统；采用μ-bar方案聚合化实现圈量子修正；以两场模型为例，分析特定势能下的有效动力学；数值求解量子修正的Friedmann方程；通过线性稳定性和动力系统分析研究全局演化行为。

Abstract: We study a multi-field model in Loop Quantum Cosmology for a maximally symmetric spacetime governed by the Einstein--Hilbert action minimally coupled to scalar fields. Using a Legendre transformation, we formulate the Hamiltonian dynamics in canonically equivalent geometrodynamical and Yang--Mills--type representations, incorporating nontrivial couplings through a geometric structure on the multi-field configuration space. Implementing the $\barμ$-scheme polymerization, we obtain the loop-quantum-corrected Friedmann equations. By focusing on the two-field model as an example, we analyze the effective dynamics for specific potentials. The \textit{quantum bouncing, transition, and slow-roll inflationary} phases are investigated numerically, and viability of the models is assessed by evaluating the number of e-folds during the inflationary phase for certain given initial conditions. The global behavior of the background evolution is further examined through linear stability and dynamical-systems analyses.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分析Simpson-Visser时空的热力学特性，特别关注正则黑洞与奇异黑洞的热力学稳定性比较，探索非线性电动力学和负动能标量场对黑洞热力学的影响。

Method: 在爱因斯坦引力耦合非线性电动力学和负动能标量场的框架下，重新推导解，使用欧几里得方法计算守恒荷，分析边界贡献，比较正则黑洞与奇异黑洞的热力学性质。

Result: 正则黑洞具有零热力学质量、守恒磁荷、单视界、有限温度和熵，满足修正的第一定律；但在相同温度磁化学势下，正则黑洞的自由能总是大于奇异黑洞，表明奇异构型在热力学上更稳定。

Conclusion: Simpson-Visser正则黑洞虽然具有正则结构和修正的热力学定律，但在热力学稳定性上不如对应的奇异黑洞，这为理解正则黑洞的热力学行为提供了新视角。

Abstract: In this work, we scrutinize the thermodynamic properties of the Simpson-Visser (SV) spacetime. Working within Einstein gravity coupled to nonlinear electrodynamics (NLED) and a scalar field with negative kinetic energy, we rederive the solution in a formulation where the integration constants do not explicitly appear in the action, allowing them to vary consistently in the thermodynamic analysis. Using the Euclidean method, we show that the regular spacetime structure modifies the boundary contributions to the conserved charge associated with time translations, allowing the NLED sector to cancel the mass term and yielding a black hole with vanishing thermodynamic mass. Nevertheless, the spacetime admits a conserved magnetic charge and describes a regular black hole with a single horizon, finite temperature, and entropy, while the first law of thermodynamics holds in a modified form. We further compare this solution with the corresponding scalar-free singular black hole obtained when the regular parameter vanishes. Placing the two configurations in the same heat bath with identical temperature and magnetic chemical potential, we find that the SV regular black hole always has a larger free energy, indicating that the scalar-free singular configuration is thermodynamically preferred.

### [164] [Gauss-Bonnet scalarization of charged qOS-black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10461)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在非线性电动力学背景下，带有高斯-博内项的爱因斯坦理论中黑洞的标量化行为，特别是研究不同参数条件下标量化的触发机制和稳定性。

Method: 在爱因斯坦-高斯-博内-标量理论框架下，采用非线性电动力学项，研究带电量子Oppenheimer-Snyder黑洞。通过分析标量耦合函数f(φ)=2λφ²，考虑质量M、作用参数α和磁荷P三个参数，探讨两种不同的高斯-博内标量化情况。

Result: 发现两种标量化类型：当α=0且λ>0时允许GB⁺标量化；当α≠0且λ<0时，在3.5653≤α≤4.6875的窄带内出现GB⁻标量化。构造了属于单分支的标量化黑洞解，标量场在视界附近非单调但在无穷远处趋于有限值。稳定性分析表明这些标量化黑洞在线性标量扰动下是稳定的。

Conclusion: 在负耦合常数λ条件下存在独特的标量化机制，产生的标量化黑洞解是稳定的，这为理解带高斯-博内项的理论中黑洞标量化现象提供了新的视角。

Abstract: The Gauss-Bonnet (GB) scalarization for charged quantum Oppenheimer-Snyder (cqOS)-black holes is investigated in the Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet-scalar theory with the nonlinear electrodynamics (NED) term. Here, the scalar coupling function to GB term is given by $f(φ)=2λφ^2$ with a coupling constant $λ$. Three parameters of mass ($M$), action parameter ($α$), and magnetic charge ($P$) are necessary to describe the cqOS-black hole, and it may become the qOS-black hole when $P=M$. The GB scalarization of cqOS-black holes comes into two cases GB$^\pm$, depending on the sign of GB term which triggers the different phenomena. For $α=0$ and $λ>0$, GB$^+$ scalarization is allowed, while for $α\not=0$ and $λ<0$, GB$^-$ scalarization appears for a narrow band of $3.5653\le α\le 4.6875$. After discussing the onset GB$^-$ scalarization, we construct scalarized qcOS-black holes which belong to the single branch. The scalar field is nonmonotonic near the horizon while it asymptotes to a finite value at infinity, indicating a distinct scalarization mechanism for negative coupling $λ$. Stability analysis shows these scalarized black holes are linearly stable under scalar perturbations.

### [165] [Energy extraction-driven instability and horizon formation in Kerr-Newman naked singularities and their limiting cases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10727)
*Vishva Patel*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文统一分析了Kerr、Reissner-Nordstrom和Kerr-Newman时空中的旋转和电磁能量提取机制，比较了效率差异，并研究了连续提取对裸奇点演化的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用粒子能量学和不可约质量形式体系，分析Kerr、Reissner-Nordstrom和Kerr-Newman时空中的能量提取。通过推导质量、自旋和电荷参数的耦合演化方程，研究连续提取过程中超极端情况的长期演化。

Result: 纯旋转提取在Kerr时空中受几何约束限制，而电磁相互作用通过有效能层扩大了负能量轨道区域，允许显著更高的提取效率。在Kerr-Newman几何中，旋转和电荷的联合效应进一步增强了可提取能量。连续提取能逐渐将裸奇点推向极端边界，对于天体物理上合理的亮度，特征演化时间尺度约为10^9年。

Conclusion: 能量提取为Reissner-Nordstrom、Kerr和Kerr-Newman裸奇点提供了不稳定的能量指示，并可能导致视界形成作为长期稳定的结果。这表明能量提取机制可能在裸奇点的演化中起到关键作用。

Abstract: Energy extraction from compact objects has been a central topic in general relativity since the introduction of the Penrose process. In this work we present a unified analysis of rotational and electromagnetic energy extraction in Kerr, Reissner-Nordstrom, and Kerr-Newman spacetimes. Using particle energetics and the irreducible mass formalism, we compare the efficiencies of these mechanisms and examine their consequences for horizonless objects. While purely rotational extraction in Kerr spacetime is fundamentally limited by geometric constraints, electromagnetic interactions enlarge the region of negative energy orbits through an effective ergoregion, allowing significantly higher efficiencies. In Kerr-Newman geometry, the combined effect of rotation and charge further enhances the extractable energy. We then study the long-term evolution of over-extremal cases under continuous extraction. By deriving coupled evolution equations for the mass, spin, and charge parameters, we show that continuous extraction can gradually drive a naked singularity toward the extremal bound. For astrophysically realistic luminosities, the characteristic evolution timescale is of order about 10^9 years. These results suggest that energy extraction provides an energetic indication of instability in Reissner-Nordstrom, Kerr, and Kerr-Newman naked singularities and may lead to horizon formation as a long-term stabilizing outcome.

This is accomplished by modelling the first-order phase transition as a turbulent fluid and employing relativistic hydrodynamic equations to estimate the required physical quantities. Two models are majorly studied for all the analysis done in this project. Also, both models contemplate the turbulence in the flow of plasma to be stationary, obeying the conditions dictated by the Kolmogorov turbulence. However, the first model uses a de-coherence function that depends on the wavenumber and time, while, the second model uses the top hat correlation, to compute the anisotropic stress. The new model introduced here adheres to the freely decaying turbulence model, but employs the time dependent de-coherence function in its computations.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有全息暗能量模型通常在视界层面现象学地引入修正的熵-面积关系，缺乏微观基础。本文旨在从微观熵函数和相应的微观态计数出发，构建一个具有坚实微观基础的扩展全息暗能量框架。

Method: 使用最近提出的双参数广义熵函数，对有界系统推导出具有两个独立面积贡献的广义全息标度熵。将此熵函数应用于全息原理，推导出包含两个不同全息扇区的广义暗能量密度。分别对哈勃视界和未来事件视界截断分析宇宙演化。

Result: 模型成功再现了物质到暗能量的转变过程。两个熵指数丰富了动力学行为，允许类精质行为或幻影机制，同时与宇宙的标准热历史保持兼容。模型自然地包含了标准全息暗能量和ΛCDM作为极限情况。

Conclusion: 基于微观熵函数的扩展全息暗能量框架提供了比现象学修正更坚实的基础，能够描述丰富的暗能量行为，同时保持与标准宇宙学历史的兼容性。

Abstract: We formulate an extended holographic dark energy scenario based on a recently proposed two-parameter generalized entropic functional. Unlike constructions that phenomenologically impose modified entropy-area relations at the horizon level, the present framework is rooted in a microscopic entropy functional and the corresponding microstate counting. For bounded systems, the entropy acquires a generalized holographic scaling with two independent area contributions, recovering the Bekenstein-Hawking entropy in the appropriate limits. Implementing this entropy within the holographic principle, we derive a generalized dark energy density containing two distinct holographic sectors, naturally embedding standard holographic dark energy and $Λ$CDM as limiting cases. We analyze the cosmological evolution for both Hubble and future event horizon cutoffs and show that the model successfully reproduces the matter-to-dark-energy transition. The two entropic exponents enrich the dynamics, allowing for quintessence-like behavior or phantom regimes, while remaining compatible with the standard thermal history of the Universe.

</details>


### [170] [Reduced phase space induced decay conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11010)
*Thomas Thiemann*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种基于约化相空间的方法来处理场论中边界条件下运动学相空间的衰减问题，通过约束的代数结构定制规范条件，将衰减条件仅施加在真实自由度上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在存在边界的场论中，需要指定场在边界上的边界条件或衰减行为。对于规范场理论，运动学相空间的衰减条件通常施加在所有场变量上，但这可能导致实际问题：约束方程可能无法代数求解，且规范自由度的衰减并非可观测量但计算泊松括号时需要。因此需要解决约束结构与运动学相空间衰减性质之间的复杂关系。

Method: 提出约化相空间诱导方法：1）根据约束的代数结构定制规范条件；2）将运动学相空间分解为规范自由度和真实自由度；3）仅对真实自由度（约化相空间）指定衰减条件；4）通过求解约束方程和规范条件，规范自由度的衰减随之确定。

Result: 该方法系统地参数化了运动学相空间的衰减条件，只需指定真实自由度的衰减，规范自由度的衰减通过求解约束和规范条件自动确定，避免了传统方法中衰减条件可能阻碍约束代数求解的问题。

Conclusion: 约化相空间诱导方法为边界条件下规范场理论的衰减问题提供了系统解决方案，通过将衰减条件仅施加在真实自由度上，简化了约束求解过程，并确保了规范不变性的明确定义。

Abstract: The definition of the phase space of field theories in presence of boundaries of Cauchy surfaces requires a choice of boundary conditions or decay behaviour of those fields. Often these conditions are motivated in part by the decay behaviour of the initial data of known exact solutions.
  In the case of gauge field theories the initial data are not free but are subject to initial value constraints. Still, the decay behaviour is commonly specified for the kinematical, i.e. unconstrained phase space. This can lead to the following practical problem: The constraints are preferably solved for field variables on which they depend only algebraically, i.e. not involving derivatives, as otherwise one would need to solve partial differential equations. However, the specified decay behaviour may prevent from doing that.
  On the other hand, a precise specification of decay for all kinematical fields appears unnecessary because the decay of gauge degrees of freedom is not observable. Yet, knowledge of their decay is required as one needs to compute Poisson brackets on the kinematical phase space in order to define what gauge invariance means. Thus the interplay between the constraint structure and the decay properties of the kinematical phase space is complex.
  In this contribution we develop a reduced phase space induced approach to the decay problem. Upon specifying gauge conditions tailored to the algebraic structure of the constraints, these define a split of the kinematical phase space into gauge and true degrees of freedom. Then the decay conditions of the kinematical phase space is systematically parametrised by a choice of decay for just the true degrees of freedom (i.e. the reduced phase space), the decay of the gauge degrees of freedom then follows unambiguously from solving both the constraints and the gauge conditions.

</details>
